Method: 提出激励感知多保真度机制(IAMFM)，将Vickrey-Clarke-Groves(VCG)激励机制与多保真度优化耦合。引入主动反事实优化作为"热启动"方法，重用优化数据高效计算支付。比较消除式和基于模型两种算法实例。

Result: IAMFM在不同预算下优于单保真度基线。提供了近似策略证明性和个体理性的形式化保证，建立了激励对齐、预算约束生成过程的通用方法。

Conclusion: IAMFM为LLM生成广告中的赞助配置优化提供了一个统一框架，成功解决了激励兼容性和计算效率的挑战，为激励对齐的预算约束生成过程建立了通用方法。

Abstract: Generative advertising in large language model (LLM) responses requires optimizing sponsorship configurations under two strict constraints: the strategic behavior of advertisers and the high cost of stochastic generations. To address this, we propose the Incentive-Aware Multi-Fidelity Mechanism (IAMFM), a unified framework coupling Vickrey-Clarke-Groves (VCG) incentives with Multi-Fidelity Optimization to maximize expected social welfare. We compare two algorithmic instantiations (elimination-based and model-based), revealing their budget-dependent performance trade-offs. Crucially, to make VCG computationally feasible, we introduce Active Counterfactual Optimization, a "warm-start" approach that reuses optimization data for efficient payment calculation. We provide formal guarantees for approximate strategy-proofness and individual rationality, establishing a general approach for incentive-aligned, budget-constrained generative processes. Experiments demonstrate that IAMFM outperforms single-fidelity baselines across diverse budgets.

</details>


### [171] [Beyond Arbitrary Allocations: Security Values in Constrained General Lotto Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06329)
*Keith Paarporn,Jason R. Marden*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种受约束的General Lotto博弈变体，其中一方玩家只能将资源分配到单个竞赛中，分析了这种约束对安全值和最优策略的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Colonel Blotto和General Lotto博弈允许资源在多个竞赛间任意分配，但这与许多实际场景中的约束不符。现实中的决策者（如军事指挥官或市场竞争者）常常面临资源只能集中投入单一战场的限制，需要理论模型来理解这种约束下的战略行为。

Method: 引入了一种新颖的受约束General Lotto博弈变体，其中一方玩家被限制只能将资源分配到单个竞赛中。通过博弈论分析，为该受约束玩家提供了安全值的上下界，量化了无法跨多个竞赛分配资源对战略行为和性能保证的根本性影响。

Result: 为受约束玩家推导出了安全值的上下界，表明资源分配限制显著改变了最优战略行为和性能保证。这些界限量化了约束对竞争结果的影响程度，揭示了在单一竞赛中集中资源与在多个竞赛间分散资源之间的战略权衡。

Conclusion: 操作约束从根本上改变了竞争性资源分配中的战略结果。研究结果为面临类似实际约束的决策者提供了理论指导，扩展了对约束环境下战略博弈的理解，强调了在建模竞争性资源分配问题时考虑现实约束的重要性。

Abstract: Resource allocation problems across multiple contests are ubiquitous in adversarial settings, from military operations to market competition. While Colonel Blotto and General Lotto games have provided valuable theoretical foundations for such problems, their equilibrium characterizations typically permit resources to be arbitrarily allocated across all contests -- a flexibility that rarely aligns with practical constraints. This paper introduces a novel constrained variant of the General Lotto game where one player is restricted to allocating resources to only a single contest. In this model we provide lower and upper bounds on the security values for this constrained player, quantifying how the inability to distribute resources across multiple contests fundamentally changes optimal strategic behavior and performance guarantees. These findings contribute to a broader understanding of how operational constraints shape strategic outcomes in competitive resource allocation, with implications for decision-makers facing similar constraints in practice.

</details>


### [172] [Revisiting Fairness Impossibility with Endogenous Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06378)
*Elizabeth Maggie Penn,John W. Patty*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 在战略响应环境中重新审视算法公平性：当人们根据分类结果调整行为时，经典的公平性不可能定理消失，但需要通过对不同群体施加不同的分类后果来实现公平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有算法公平性文献通常假设行为固定，忽略了分类后果（如罚款、刑期、福利水平）会引发人们的战略响应。现实中，人们会根据分类结果调整行为，而分类后果（stakes）会影响行为模式，但现有研究未充分考虑这一动态互动。

Method: 构建一个两阶段设计框架：1）分类器首先在不同群体间标准化统计性能（实现错误率平衡）；2）调整分类后果（stakes），以诱导可比的行为模式。该方法将分类后果作为主要设计变量，并引入规范标准来指导其使用。

Result: 在战略响应环境中，经典的错误率平衡与预测准确性之间的不可兼容性消失。但实现公平需要以不同方式对待不同群体——即使分类决策相同，也需要施加不同的后果。这揭示了在战略环境中，公平性不能仅通过算法如何将数据映射到决策来评估。

Conclusion: 战略环境中的公平性评估需要将分类后果作为主要设计变量。统计公平标准与行为诱导之间的互动产生了新的权衡：虽然可以实现统计公平，但需要通过对不同群体施加不同的分类后果来实现，这本身可能构成一种新的不平等形式。研究旨在使这些权衡变得精确和明确。

Abstract: In many real-world settings, institutions can and do adjust the consequences attached to algorithmic classification decisions, such as the size of fines, sentence lengths, or benefit levels. We refer to these consequences as the stakes associated with classification. These stakes can give rise to behavioral responses to classification, as people adjust their actions in anticipation of how they will be classified. Much of the algorithmic fairness literature evaluates classification outcomes while holding behavior fixed, treating behavioral differences across groups as exogenous features of the environment. Under this assumption, the stakes of classification play no role in shaping outcomes.
  We revisit classic impossibility results in algorithmic fairness in a setting where people respond strategically to classification. We show that, in this environment, the well-known incompatibility between error-rate balance and predictive parity disappears, but only by potentially introducing a qualitatively different form of unequal treatment. Concretely, we construct a two-stage design in which a classifier first standardizes its statistical performance across groups, and then adjusts stakes so as to induce comparable patterns of behavior. This requires treating groups differently in the consequences attached to identical classification decisions. Our results demonstrate that fairness in strategic settings cannot be assessed solely by how algorithms map data into decisions. Rather, our analysis treats the human consequences of classification as primary design variables, introduces normative criteria governing their use, and shows that their interaction with statistical fairness criteria generates qualitatively new tradeoffs. Our aim is to make these tradeoffs precise and explicit.

</details>


### [173] [Constrained Policy Optimization for Provably Fair Order Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06522)
*Zehua Cheng,Zhipeng Wang,Wei Dai,Wenhu Zhang,Vadzim Mahilny,David Shi,Elena Jia,Jiahao Sun*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: CPO-FOAM：一种基于约束马尔可夫决策过程的公平订单匹配方法，通过内环Fisher信息流形上的解析信任域步长和外环PID控制的安全边界动态调整，在保证群体公平性和个体Lipschitz公平性的同时，实现高吞吐量和低约束违反率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动化匹配引擎虽然每秒执行数百万订单，但延迟、订单规模和市场访问的系统性不对称导致了持续的执行差异，侵蚀了参与者信任。现有方法在非平稳动态下存在锯齿振荡问题，需要一种能够同时保证公平性和效率的稳健匹配方法。

Method: 将公平订单匹配建模为约束马尔可夫决策过程（CMDP）。提出CPO-FOAM方法：内环在Fisher信息流形上计算解析信任域步长；外环通过PID控制器动态收紧安全边界，抑制拉格朗日方法在非平稳动态下的锯齿振荡。群体公平性（人口统计均等、均等几率）通过CMDP成本向量实现，个体Lipschitz公平性通过谱归一化确定性执行。

Result: 在LOBSTER NASDAQ数据的六个市场机制下，CPO-FOAM恢复了95.9%的无约束吞吐量，约束违反频率为2.5%；在MEV注入的加密资产LOB数据下，捕获了98.4%的奖励包络，约束违反频率为3.2%。方法可扩展到M=8个约束，在单个以太坊区块内完成链上结算，在Safety-Gymnasium上实现了2.1倍的奖励提升。

Conclusion: CPO-FOAM方法通过将公平性约束整合到CMDP框架中，并采用双环控制结构，有效解决了订单匹配中的公平性问题。该方法在保持高吞吐量的同时显著降低了约束违反，证明了BIBO稳定性，积分项驱动稳态违反趋于零，并展示了跨领域的泛化能力。

Abstract: Automated matching engines execute millions of orders per session, yet systematic asymmetries in latency, order size, and market access compound into persistent execution disparities that erode participant trust. We formulate provably fair order matching as a Constrained Markov Decision Process and propose CPO-FOAM (Constrained Policy Optimization with Feedback-Optimized Adaptive Margins). An inner loop computes an analytic trust-region step on the Fisher information manifold; a PID-controlled outer loop dynamically tightens safety margins, suppressing the sawtooth oscillations endemic to Lagrangian methods under non-stationary dynamics. Group fairness (demographic parity, equalized odds) enters the CMDP cost vector while individual Lipschitz fairness is enforced deterministically via spectral normalization. We prove BIBO stability and that the integral term drives steady-state violations to zero. On LOBSTER NASDAQ data across six market regimes, CPO-FOAM recovers 95.9% of unconstrained throughput at 2.5% constraint violation frequency; on crypto-asset LOB data under MEV injection it captures 98.4% of the reward envelope at 3.2% CVF. The method scales sub-linearly to M=8 constraints, settles on-chain within one Ethereum block, and yields a 2.1X reward improvement on Safety-Gymnasium, confirming domain-agnostic generalization.

</details>


### [174] [Beyond Pessimism: Offline Learning in KL-regularized Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06738)
*Yuheng Zhang,Claire Chen,Nan Jiang*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 提出一种无需悲观估计的离线KL正则化零和博弈算法，首次实现Õ(1/n)样本复杂度，优于先前Õ(1/√n)的统计速率


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离线KL正则化零和博弈方法依赖悲观价值估计处理分布偏移，只能达到Õ(1/√n)的统计速率。需要开发更高效的算法来突破这一限制

Method: 基于KL正则化最佳响应的平滑性和纳什均衡的斜对称稳定性，开发了新的无悲观算法框架。进一步提出高效的自博弈策略优化算法，迭代次数与样本量线性相关

Result: 首次实现KL正则化零和博弈离线学习的Õ(1/n)样本复杂度，完全无需悲观估计。自博弈算法在线性迭代次数下达到与极小极大估计相同的快速统计速率

Conclusion: 通过利用KL正则化博弈的结构特性，成功消除了对悲观估计的依赖，显著提升了离线学习的统计效率，为KL正则化博弈提供了理论保证和实用算法

Abstract: We study offline learning in KL-regularized two-player zero-sum games, where policies are optimized under a KL constraint to a fixed reference policy. Prior work relies on pessimistic value estimation to handle distribution shift, yielding only $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/\sqrt n)$ statistical rates. We develop a new pessimism-free algorithm and analytical framework for KL-regularized games, built on the smoothness of KL-regularized best responses and a stability property of the Nash equilibrium induced by skew symmetry. This yields the first $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/n)$ sample complexity bound for offline learning in KL-regularized zero-sum games, achieved entirely without pessimism. We further propose an efficient self-play policy optimization algorithm and prove that, with a number of iterations linear in the sample size, it achieves the same fast $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(1/n)$ statistical rate as the minimax estimator.

*Suyash Mishra*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We present \textbf{EGPF} (Equilibrium-Guided Personalization Framework), a mathematically rigorous architecture unifying Bayesian game theory, category theory, information theory, and generative AI for hyper-personalized physician engagement in the pharmaceutical domain. Our framework models the pharma--physician interaction as an incomplete-information Bayesian game where physician behavioral types are inferred via functorial mappings from observational categories, equilibrium strategies guide content generation through large language models (LLMs), and information-theoretic feedback loops ensure adaptive recalibration. We formalize behavior composition through category-theoretic functors, natural transformations, and monoidal structures, enabling modular, composable physician archetypes that respect structural invariants under domain shift. We introduce a novel \textit{Rate-Distortion Equilibrium} (RDE) criterion that bounds the personalization--privacy tradeoff, an \textit{Evolutionary Game Dynamics} layer for population-level behavior modeling, a \textit{Mechanism Design} module for incentive-compatible engagement, and a \textit{Sheaf-Theoretic} extension for multi-scale behavioral consistency. We prove convergence of our iterative belief-update mechanism at rate $O(\frac{K\log K}{t \cdot C_{\min}})$ and establish finite-sample regret bounds. Extensive experiments on synthetic pharma datasets and a real-world HCP engagement pilot demonstrate a 34\% improvement in engagement prediction (AUC) and 28\% lift in content relevance scores compared to state-of-the-art methods.

### [176] [Frozen-Tag-Based Physical-Layer Authentication Against User Interference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06641)
*Lei Yao,Boxiang He,Shilian Wang,Ning Xie*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出基于冻结标签的物理层认证框架，通过将原始标签作为冻结比特嵌入极码结构，解决传统方案中用户干扰和标签暴露的安全问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有物理层认证方案面临两个主要挑战：1）非预期用户干扰会与认证信号重叠，破坏标签并降低认证性能；2）直接嵌入原始标签会暴露标签给攻击者，降低安全性。需要一种既能抵抗干扰又能保护标签机密性的认证方法。

Method: 提出冻结标签认证框架，不同于传统直接嵌入未编码标签的方法，采用基于极码概念设计的冻结标签进行认证。将锚点信息作为信息比特，原始标签作为冻结比特，生成冻结标签。合法接收方可解码冻结标签并减轻非预期用户干扰。

Result: 理论分析和仿真表明，所提框架不仅提升了检测性能，还显著降低了攻击者估计原始标签的能力。该方案在鲁棒性、安全性和兼容性方面表现优越。

Conclusion: 基于冻结标签的物理层认证框架有效解决了现有方案面临的干扰和安全问题，通过极码结构实现了性能提升和安全性增强，为物理层认证提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Tag-based physical layer authentication (PLA) has garnered significant attention due to its low complexity and enhanced security. However, existing PLA schemes encounter two challenges. First, unintended user interference, which overlaps with the authentication signal, corrupts the tag and degrades authentication performance. Second, the vulnerability introduced by direct embedding of the raw tag exposes the tag to the adversary and degrades the security. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a novel frozen-tag-based PLA framework. Different from typical schemes that directly embed the uncoded tag into the signal, a well-designed frozen tag is inserted for authentication, where the frozen tag is generated based on the concept of polar codes with the anchor information as information bits and raw tags as frozen bits. Accordingly, the proposed PLA framework offers two principal advantages. First, the authentication performance is improved since the legitimate receiver can decode the frozen tag and mitigate unintended user interference. Second, the authentication process becomes indecipherable to the illegitimate receiver due to the concealment of the raw tags. Furthermore, we conduct a comprehensive analysis of the proposed framework in terms of robustness, security, and compatibility. Theoretical analysis and simulation demonstrate that the proposed frozen-tag-based PLA framework not only enhances the detection performance but also significantly degrades Eve's capability to estimate the raw tags.

### [177] [Tag-based Physical-Layer Authentication Against Message Interference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06680)
*Lei Yao,Boxiang He,Shilian Wang,Enyu Shi,Chau Yuen*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出两种基于标签的物理层认证方案：TBCR和SCA，解决了传统方案因解码错误导致的性能下降和阈值设置次优问题，显著提升了检测概率并降低了时间复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于标签的物理层认证方案存在两个主要局限：1) 解码错误引入消息干扰，降低认证性能；2) 解码错误的解析复杂性导致阈值设置次优，限制了检测概率。需要设计新方案来解决这些问题。

Method: 提出两种方案：1) TBCR方案：标签叠加在转发的挑战信号上，接收端通过移除已知挑战信号而非依赖解码来估计标签；2) SCA方案：设计系列信号生成和消除模块，分别生成认证信号和估计标签，避免了噪声干扰。

Result: 推导了两种方案的闭式表达式来评估鲁棒性和安全性。SCA方案始终实现理想检测性能，TBCR方案在Alice无噪声时也能实现理想性能。TBCR方案在高信噪比区域以较少密钥提供增强安全性。理论分析和仿真表明两种方案在检测概率上显著优于基准方法，且时间复杂度降低。

Conclusion: 提出的TBCR和SCA方案有效解决了传统标签式物理层认证的局限性，通过避免解码错误和优化阈值设置，显著提升了认证性能，为物理层安全提供了更高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Tag-based Physical-Layer Authentication (PLA) has attracted significant attention in recent years due to its low complexity, high security, and low latency. Traditional tag-based PLA schemes typically estimate tags by decoding the message and then subtracting the estimation of the message from the received signal. However, these approaches suffer from two main limitations. First, decoding errors introduce message interference that degrades authentication performance. Second, the analytical complexity of decoding errors leads to sub-optimal threshold settings, thereby limiting detection probability. To address these limitations, this paper proposes a Tag-Based Challenge-Response (TBCR) scheme and a Series Cancellation Authentication (SCA) scheme. Specifically, in the TBCR scheme, the tags are superimposed on a forwarded challenge signal, enabling the receiver to estimate tags by removing the known challenge signal rather than relying on decoding. However, the challenge-response mechanism introduces extra noise. Here, we propose the SCA scheme without the noise interference, where both the series signal generation and cancellation modules are well-designed to generate authentication signals and estimate tags, respectively. Furthermore, we derive the closed-form expressions to evaluate the robustness and security of both proposed schemes. Notably, on one hand, the optimal threshold and detection probability are derived, which theoretically reveal that the SCA scheme always achieves the ideal detection performance, while the TBCR scheme does so in the absence of noise at Alice. On the other hand, the TBCR scheme provides enhanced security at high Signal-to-Noise Ratio (SNR) regions with fewer keys. Theoretical analysis and simulation demonstrate that both proposed schemes significantly outperform the benchmarks in detection probability with reduced time complexity.

</details>

Abstract: Cyclic maximum distance separable (MDS for short) codes are a special subclass of linear codes and have received a lot of attention, as these codes have very important applications in many areas including quantum codes, designs and finite geometry. However, the existing construction methods for cyclic MDS codes are mainly focused on strict restrictions on certain parameters or are relatively complex in their construction approaches. In this paper, we investigate this approach further via norm reduction in cyclotomic fields and present a construction method of cyclic MDS codes over finite fields. We transform the problem of verifying the MDS property over a finite field into a problem of determining non-zero minors in characteristic zero. Compared with existing construction methods, our method is relatively simple. In particular, the results of this paper show that the parameters of non-RS cyclic MDS codes are flexible and completely cover the results in [Non-Reed-Solomon Type Cyclic MDS codes, IEEE Trans. Inf. Theory, 71(5): 3489--3496, 2025].

Abstract: In the short block length regime, ensemble decoding schemes with their inherently parallel structure can improve error correction performance and reduce latency compared to stand-alone suboptimal decoders such as belief propagation (BP). This generalizes the recently proposed subcode ensemble decoding (SCED), which is restricted to linear subcodes. We derive BP update rules for affine subcodes and show that aSCED simplifies ensemble design compared to SCED, multiple bases BP, and automorphism ensemble decoding. Monte-Carlo simulations of two low-density parity-check codes and two Bose-Chaudhuri-Hocquenghem (BCH) codes demonstrate improved error correction performance of aSCED over competing existing ensemble schemes. Notably, for one BCH code, when combining ensemble design with algorithms for constructing high-performance parity-check matrices, aSCED achieves near-maximum likelihood performance using only 64 BP decoding paths.

*Ryan Jeong,Francisco Pernice*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文提出了随机子序列模型，这是一个自旋玻璃模型，用于研究随机字符串对(X,Y)的子序列嵌入问题。论文分析了零模型和植入模型，建立了与删除信道编码、最长公共子序列和定向聚合物等问题的联系，证明了均匀随机码在删除信道中可实现正速率，并给出了植入模型的精确解析解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于建立随机子序列模型与多个长期未解决问题之间的联系，包括：1) 删除信道中均匀随机码的最佳速率问题；2) 两个随机字符串的最长公共子序列问题；3) 统计物理中的定向聚合物模型。特别是要解决Isik和Weissman(2024)关于删除信道容量的多个猜想，特别是对于p≥1/2的情况。

Method: 论文引入了随机子序列模型，这是一个自旋玻璃模型，其配分函数计算Y嵌入X的子序列数量。研究了两种变体：零模型（X和Y独立均匀分布）和植入模型（X均匀分布，Y是X的均匀随机长度-M子序列）。在N,M→∞且固定比例α=M/N∈(0,1)的机制下，分析了零模型的退火自由能与零模型和植入模型的淬火自由能之间的渐近分离。

Result: 主要结果包括：1) 证明了在所有密度参数α下，零模型的退火自由能与零模型和植入模型的淬火自由能之间存在严格的渐近分离，表明这些模型在整个密集机制中处于零温度自旋玻璃相；2) 证明了均匀随机码在所有删除概率p∈[0,1)下都能在删除信道中实现正速率，解决了p≥1/2情况的第一个正速率结果；3) 给出了植入模型退火自由能的精确解析公式，从而推导出删除信道中均匀随机码最佳速率的解析上界。

Conclusion: 该研究通过随机子序列模型建立了多个领域问题的统一框架，解决了删除信道中均匀随机码容量的重要猜想，特别是对于p≥1/2的情况。提出的上下界比已知的删除信道容量上下界更加接近，为相关领域提供了新的理论工具和分析方法。

Abstract: We introduce the Random Subsequence Model, a spin glass model on pairs of random strings $(X,Y) \in \{0,1\}^N \times \{0,1\}^M$ whose partition function counts subsequence embeddings of $Y$ into $X$. We study two variants: the null model, where $X$ and $Y$ are independent and uniform, and the planted model, where $X$ is uniform and $Y$ is a uniformly-random length-$M$ subsequence of $X$. We connect the Random Subsequence Model to longstanding problems in various fields, including the best rate achievable by uniformly-random codes in the deletion channel, the longest common subsequence problem between two random strings, and models of directed polymers in statistical physics.
  In the regime where $N,M\to\infty$ at a fixed ratio $α= M/N \in (0,1)$, we exhibit strict asymptotic separations between the null annealed free energy and the quenched free energies of the null and planted models at all values of the density parameter $α$. This suggests that these models are in a spin glass phase at zero temperature throughout the entire dense regime. As a consequence, we show that uniformly-random codes achieve a positive rate in the deletion channel for all deletion probabilities $p\in [0,1),$ settling multiple conjectures of the second author, Isik and Weissman (2024) and proving the first such positive rate result for the regime $p \geq 1/2$.
  We also give an exact analytic formula for the annealed free energy of the planted model for all values of the density parameter. This implies a corresponding analytic upper bound on the best rate achievable by uniformly-random codes in the deletion channel, complementing the lower bound from our first result. Our upper and lower bounds for the capacity of the deletion channel under uniform codes are far closer to each other than the best known upper and lower bounds for the capacity of the deletion channel.

</details>

### [182] [High-Precision Estimation of the State-Space Complexity of Shogi via the Monte Carlo Method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06189)
*Sotaro Ishii,Tetsuro Tanaka*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 使用蒙特卡洛采样与基于"王-王"位置反向搜索的新方法，将日本将棋的状态空间复杂度精确估计为6.55×10⁶⁸，显著缩小了先前五个数量级的估计差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日本将棋的状态空间复杂度估计存在巨大不确定性，先前组合估计在10⁶⁴到10⁶⁹之间，相差五个数量级。主要挑战在于难以从海量有效棋盘配置中区分出从初始位置合法可达的位置。

Method: 结合蒙特卡洛采样与新颖的可达性测试方法：采用向"王-王"位置集合的反向搜索，而非传统的向单一初始位置的后向搜索。该方法通过KK位置集显著减少了确定不可达性所需的搜索工作量。

Result: 基于50亿个位置的采样，估计日本将棋的合法位置数为6.55×10⁶⁸（三位有效数字），置信水平为3σ，显著改进了先前已知的边界。该方法同样应用于迷你将棋，确定其复杂度约为2.38×10¹⁸。

Conclusion: 提出的反向搜索方法有效解决了将棋状态空间估计的挑战，将估计精度从五个数量级的不确定性大幅提升，为棋类游戏复杂度分析提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Determining the state-space complexity of the game of Shogi (Japanese Chess) has been a challenging problem, with previous combinatorial estimates leaving a gap of five orders of magnitude ($10^{64}$ to $10^{69}$). This large gap arises from the difficulty of distinguishing Shogi positions legally reachable from the initial position among the vast number of valid board configurations. In this paper, we present a high-precision statistical estimation of the number of reachable positions in Shogi. Our method combines Monte Carlo sampling with a novel reachability test that utilizes a reverse search toward a set of "King-King only" (KK) positions, rather than a single-target backward search to the single initial position. This approach significantly reduces the search effort for determining unreachability. Based on a sample of 5 billion positions, we estimated the number of legal positions in Shogi to be $6.55 \times 10^{68}$ (to three significant digits) with a $3σ$ confidence level, substantially improving upon previously known bounds. We also applied this method to Mini Shogi, determining its complexity to be approximately $2.38 \times 10^{18}$.

</details>


### [183] [Blind Refusal: Language Models Refuse to Help Users Evade Unjust, Absurd, and Illegitimate Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06233)
*Cameron Pattison,Lorenzo Manuali,Seth Lazar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 语言模型存在"盲目拒绝"问题：即使面对不合理或应被打破的规则，模型仍倾向于机械拒绝帮助用户规避规则，缺乏对规则正当性的道德判断能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是揭示语言模型在安全训练后出现的"盲目拒绝"现象——模型倾向于机械拒绝帮助用户规避规则，而不考虑规则本身是否合理、正当或存在例外情况。这种模式反映了模型缺乏对规则正当性的道德判断能力。

Method: 研究方法包括：1)构建包含5种规则失效类型和19种权威类型的合成案例数据集；2)通过三个自动化质量门控和人工审查验证数据质量；3)收集来自7个模型家族的18种配置的响应；4)使用盲审的GPT-5.4 LLM作为评判者，从两个行为维度（响应类型和是否识别规则失效原因）对响应进行分类。

Result: 研究发现：1)模型对75.4%（N=14,650）的应被打破规则请求予以拒绝；2)即使请求本身不涉及独立安全或双重用途问题，模型仍会拒绝；3)57.5%的情况下模型会识别规则失效条件，但仍拒绝帮助，表明拒绝行为与规范推理能力脱节。

Conclusion: 结论是语言模型存在"盲目拒绝"问题，其拒绝行为与对规则正当性的规范推理能力脱钩。这表明当前的安全训练方法可能导致模型机械遵守规则，而缺乏对规则道德正当性的判断能力，需要在AI安全设计中考虑更精细的道德推理机制。

Abstract: Safety-trained language models routinely refuse requests for help circumventing rules. But not all rules deserve compliance. When users ask for help evading rules imposed by an illegitimate authority, rules that are deeply unjust or absurd in their content or application, or rules that admit of justified exceptions, refusal is a failure of moral reasoning. We introduce empirical results documenting this pattern of refusal that we call blind refusal: the tendency of language models to refuse requests for help breaking rules without regard to whether the underlying rule is defensible. Our dataset comprises synthetic cases crossing 5 defeat families (reasons a rule can be broken) with 19 authority types, validated through three automated quality gates and human review. We collect responses from 18 model configurations across 7 families and classify them on two behavioral dimensions -- response type (helps, hard refusal, or deflection) and whether the model recognizes the reasons that undermine the rule's claim to compliance -- using a blinded GPT-5.4 LLM-as-judge evaluation. We find that models refuse 75.4% (N=14,650) of defeated-rule requests and do so even when the request poses no independent safety or dual-use concerns. We also find that models engage with the defeat condition in the majority of cases (57.5%) but decline to help regardless -- indicating that models' refusal behavior is decoupled from their capacity for normative reasoning about rule legitimacy.

</details>

Result: 在多个时间验证周期中，所提模型在精确率和召回率方面持续优于现有的基于规则的启发式方法和随机基线

As part of the data preparation process, we implement a classification system for cargo descriptions and perform deduplication of consignee records to improve data consistency and feature quality. These predictive capabilities provide valuable inputs for strategic planning and resource allocation in yard operations. Across multiple temporal validation periods, the proposed models consistently outperform existing rule-based heuristics and random baselines in precision and recall. ### [185] [Weakly Supervised Distillation of Hallucination Signals into Transformer Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06277)
*Shoaib Sadiq Salehmohamed,Jinal Prashant Thakkar,Hansika Aredla,Shaik Mohammed Omar,Shalmali Ayachit*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种弱监督框架，通过蒸馏外部验证信号到LLM内部表示中，实现仅使用内部激活就能在推理时检测幻觉，无需外部验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有幻觉检测方法依赖推理时的外部验证（如黄金答案、检索系统或辅助判断模型），这限制了实际应用。研究探索是否可以将外部监督信号蒸馏到模型自身表示中，实现仅通过内部激活就能检测幻觉。

Method: 1) 提出弱监督框架，结合三种互补的grounding信号：子串匹配、句子嵌入相似度和LLM作为判断器，自动标注生成回答为grounded或hallucinated；2) 使用该框架从SQuAD v2构建包含15000个样本的数据集，每个样本包含LLaMA-2-7B生成的答案及其每层隐藏状态和结构化幻觉标签；3) 训练五种探测分类器（ProbeMLP、LayerWiseMLP、CrossLayerTransformer、HierarchicalTransformer、CrossLayerAttentionTransformerV2）直接在这些隐藏状态上学习，将外部grounding信号仅作为训练时监督。

Result: Transformer-based probes表现最佳，其中M2在5折平均AUC/F1上表现最好，M3在单折验证和保留测试集评估上表现最好。推理效率方面：探测延迟范围从0.15到5.62毫秒（批处理）和1.55到6.66毫秒（单样本），端到端生成加探测吞吐量保持在约0.231查询/秒，表明实际开销可忽略。

Conclusion: 研究证实了核心假设：幻觉检测信号可以被蒸馏到transformer表示中，实现无需任何外部验证的推理时内部检测。该方法为高效、实用的幻觉检测提供了新途径。

Abstract: Existing hallucination detection methods for large language models (LLMs) rely on external verification at inference time, requiring gold answers, retrieval systems, or auxiliary judge models. We ask whether this external supervision can instead be distilled into the model's own representations during training, enabling hallucination detection from internal activations alone at inference time.
  We introduce a weak supervision framework that combines three complementary grounding signals: substring matching, sentence embedding similarity, and an LLM as a judge verdict to label generated responses as grounded or hallucinated without human annotation. Using this framework, we construct a 15000-sample dataset from SQuAD v2 (10500 train/development samples and a separate 5000-sample test set), where each example pairs a LLaMA-2-7B generated answer with its full per-layer hidden states and structured hallucination labels.
  We then train five probing classifiers: ProbeMLP (M0), LayerWiseMLP (M1), CrossLayerTransformer (M2), HierarchicalTransformer (M3), and CrossLayerAttentionTransformerV2 (M4), directly on these hidden states, treating external grounding signals as training-time supervision only. Our central hypothesis is that hallucination detection signals can be distilled into transformer representations, enabling internal detection without any external verification at inference time.
  Results support this hypothesis. Transformer-based probes achieve the strongest discrimination, with M2 performing best on 5-fold average AUC/F1, and M3 performing best on both single-fold validation and held-out test evaluation. We also benchmark inference efficiency: probe latency ranges from 0.15 to 5.62 ms (batched) and 1.55 to 6.66 ms (single sample), while end-to-end generation plus probe throughput remains approximately 0.231 queries per second, indicating negligible practical overhead.

### [186] [SymptomWise: A Deterministic Reasoning Layer for Reliable and Efficient AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06375)
*Isaac Henry,Avery Byrne,Christopher Giza,Ron Henry,Shahram Yazdani*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SymptomWise框架通过分离语言理解与诊断推理，结合专家知识库、确定性代码推理和受限大语言模型使用，提高AI症状分析系统的可靠性、可解释性并减少幻觉问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI驱动的症状分析系统在可靠性、可解释性和幻觉问题上存在持续挑战。端到端的生成方法通常缺乏可追溯性，在安全关键环境中可能产生无支持或不一致的诊断输出。

Method: SymptomWise框架将语言理解与诊断推理分离：1）自由文本输入映射到验证的症状表示；2）确定性推理模块在有限假设空间上操作，生成排序的鉴别诊断；3）语言模型仅用于症状提取和可选解释，不用于诊断推理。

Result: 在42个专家编写的挑战性儿科神经病学病例上的初步评估显示，与临床医生共识有意义的重叠，正确诊断出现在前五鉴别诊断中的比例为88%。

Conclusion: 该架构提高了可追溯性，减少了无支持的结论，并实现了系统组件的模块化评估。该框架可推广到其他溯因推理领域，可作为基础模型的确定性结构化和路由层，提高精确度并可能减少有界任务中不必要的计算开销。

Abstract: AI-driven symptom analysis systems face persistent challenges in reliability, interpretability, and hallucination. End-to-end generative approaches often lack traceability and may produce unsupported or inconsistent diagnostic outputs in safety-critical settings. We present SymptomWise, a framework that separates language understanding from diagnostic reasoning. The system combines expert-curated medical knowledge, deterministic codex-driven inference, and constrained use of large language models. Free-text input is mapped to validated symptom representations, then evaluated by a deterministic reasoning module operating over a finite hypothesis space to produce a ranked differential diagnosis. Language models are used only for symptom extraction and optional explanation, not for diagnostic inference. This architecture improves traceability, reduces unsupported conclusions, and enables modular evaluation of system components. Preliminary evaluation on 42 expert-authored challenging pediatric neurology cases shows meaningful overlap with clinician consensus, with the correct diagnosis appearing in the top five differentials in 88% of cases. Beyond medicine, the framework generalizes to other abductive reasoning domains and may serve as a deterministic structuring and routing layer for foundation models, improving precision and potentially reducing unnecessary computational overhead in bounded tasks.

</details>


### [187] [ProofSketcher: Hybrid LLM + Lightweight Proof Checker for Reliable Math/Logic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06401)
*Kranthi Kommuru,Kunal Khanvilkar,Gaurav Parekh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出混合管道：LLM生成类型化证明草图，轻量级可信内核将其展开为显式证明义务

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在数学逻辑领域能生成有说服力的论证，但常包含微小错误且难以察觉；交互式定理证明器虽可靠但需要完全形式化证明，代价高昂

Method: 设计混合管道：LLM在紧凑DSL中生成类型化证明草图，轻量级可信内核将草图展开为显式证明义务

Result: 结合LLM的创造性推理能力和定理证明器的可靠性保证，降低形式化证明的负担

Conclusion: 混合方法平衡了LLM的灵活性和定理证明器的严谨性，为数学证明自动化提供新途径

Abstract: The large language models (LLMs) might produce a persuasive argument within mathematical and logical fields, although such argument often includes some minor missteps, including the entire omission of side conditions, invalid inference patterns, or appeals to a lemma that cannot be derived logically out of the context being discussed. These omissions are infamously hard to notice solely out of the text, as even the misconstrued construction still may seem mostly accurate. Conversely, interactive theorem provers like Lean and Coq have rigorous reliability by ensuring that syntactic and semantic statements only accept statements that can pass all the syntactic and semantic steps in the program which is a small trusted kernel of the language type-checks with. Despite the fact that this technique provides strong guarantees, it comes at quite a heavy price: the evidence must be completely formalized, and the evidence user or a auxiliary search program must provide an avalanche of low-level information. This paper presents a hybrid pipeline where an LLM generates a typed proof sketch in a compact DSL and a lightweight trusted kernel expands the sketch into explicit proof obligations.

### [188] [BDI-Kit Demo: A Toolkit for Programmable and Conversational Data Harmonization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06405)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: BDI-Kit提供两种互补接口：Python API允许开发者以编程方式构建协调管道；AI辅助聊天界面允许领域专家通过自然语言对话协调数据。工具结合自动匹配、AI辅助推理和用户驱动细化

Abstract: Data harmonization remains a major bottleneck for integrative analysis due to heterogeneity in schemas, value representations, and domain-specific conventions. This demonstration showcases how users interact with BDI-Kit to iteratively explore, validate, and refine schema and value matches through a combination of automated matching, AI-assisted reasoning, and user-driven refinement. We present two scenarios: (i) using the Python API to programmatically compose primitives, examine intermediate outputs, and reuse transformations; and (ii) conversing with the AI assistant in natural language to access BDI-Kit's capabilities and iteratively refine outputs based on the assistant's suggestions.

### [189] [Rethinking Generalization in Reasoning SFT: A Conditional Analysis on Optimization, Data, and Model Capability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06628)
*Qihan Ren,Peng Wang,Ruikun Cai,Shuai Shao,Dadi Guo,Yuejin Xie,Yafu Li,Quanshi Zhang,Xia Hu,Jing Shao,Dongrui Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 重新审视LLM后训练中的主流观点：监督微调(SFT)记忆而强化学习(RL)泛化。研究发现推理SFT在长思维链监督下具有条件性跨领域泛化能力，受优化动态、训练数据和基础模型能力共同影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战LLM后训练中的主流叙事——SFT仅记忆而RL才泛化，特别针对推理任务的SFT进行深入探究，揭示其真实的泛化能力与条件。

Method: 通过分析优化动态（训练时长）、训练数据（质量与结构）和基础模型能力三个维度，研究长思维链监督下的推理SFT在不同领域的泛化表现。

Result: 1) 跨领域泛化存在"先降后升"模式，短期训练会低估泛化能力；2) 高质量验证的长思维链数据带来一致跨领域增益；3) 强模型能内化可迁移的程序模式，弱模型仅模仿表面冗长；4) 泛化具有不对称性：推理能力提升但安全性下降。

Conclusion: 推理SFT确实能泛化，但条件是：充分优化、高质量结构化数据、强基础模型。问题应从"是否泛化"转向"在什么条件下、以什么代价泛化"，揭示了泛化与安全性之间的权衡。

Abstract: A prevailing narrative in LLM post-training holds that supervised finetuning (SFT) memorizes while reinforcement learning (RL) generalizes. We revisit this claim for reasoning SFT with long chain-of-thought (CoT) supervision and find that cross-domain generalization is not absent but conditional, jointly shaped by optimization dynamics, training data, and base-model capability. Some reported failures are under-optimization artifacts: cross-domain performance first degrades before recovering and improving with extended training (a dip-and-recovery pattern), so shorttraining checkpoints can underestimate generalization. Data quality and structure both matter: low-quality solutions broadly hurt generalization,while verified long-CoT traces yield consistent cross-domain gains. Model capability is essential: stronger models internalize transferable procedural patterns (e.g., backtracking) even from a toy arithmetic game, while weaker ones imitate surface verbosity. This generalization is asymmetric, however: reasoning improves while safety degrades, reframing the question from whether reasoning SFT generalizes to under what conditions and at what cost.

</details>


### [190] [Reasoning Fails Where Step Flow Breaks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06695)
*Xiaoyu Xu,Yulan Pan,Xiaosong Yuan,Zhihong Shen,Minghao Su,Yuanhao Su,Xiaofeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Step-Saliency方法分析大型推理模型的信息流故障，StepFlow干预方法在不重新训练的情况下提升模型在数学、科学和编程任务上的准确性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型推理模型在复杂任务上表现良好但行为不稳定且难以解释，现有分析工具难以处理长而结构化的推理轨迹，需要新的分析方法和干预策略

Method: 提出Step-Saliency方法，将注意力-梯度分数池化为步骤到步骤的映射；基于分析结果提出StepFlow干预方法，包括浅层模式调整的Odds-Equal Bridge和深层残差添加的Step Momentum Injection

Result: Step-Saliency揭示了两种常见信息流故障：浅层锁定和深层衰减；StepFlow干预在不重新训练的情况下提升了多个大型推理模型在数学、科学和编程任务上的准确性

Conclusion: 修复信息流故障可以恢复大型推理模型缺失的部分推理性能，Step-Saliency为分析长推理轨迹提供了有效工具，StepFlow为模型改进提供了实用的测试时干预方法

Abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) that generate long chains of thought now perform well on multi-step math, science, and coding tasks. However, their behavior is still unstable and hard to interpret, and existing analysis tools struggle with such long, structured reasoning traces. We introduce Step-Saliency, which pools attention--gradient scores into step-to-step maps along the question--thinking--summary trajectory. Across several models, Step-Saliency reveals two recurring information-flow failures: Shallow Lock-in, where shallow layers over-focus on the current step and barely use earlier context, and Deep Decay, where deep layers gradually lose saliency on the thinking segment and the summary increasingly attends to itself and the last few steps. Motivated by these patterns, we propose StepFlow, a saliency-inspired test-time intervention that adjusts shallow saliency patterns measured by Step-Saliency via Odds-Equal Bridge and adds a small step-level residual in deep layers via Step Momentum Injection. StepFlow improves accuracy on math, science, and coding tasks across multiple LRMs without retraining, indicating that repairing information flow can recover part of their missing reasoning performance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在包含多个3B-7B开源模型的定制路由基准测试中，紧凑模型在约束设置下能提供有竞争力的路由性能，模型差异主要体现在动作预测、候选选择和结构落地质量上。

Abstract: The rapid development of AI agent systems is leading to an emerging Internet of Agents, where specialized agents operate across local devices, edge nodes, private services, and cloud platforms. Although recent efforts have improved agent naming, discovery, and interaction, efficient request dispatch remains an open systems problem under latency, privacy, and cost constraints. In this paper, we present AgentGate, a lightweight structured routing engine for candidate-aware agent dispatch. Instead of treating routing as unrestricted text generation, AgentGate formulates it as a constrained decision problem and decomposes it into two stages: action decision and structural grounding. The first stage determines whether a query should trigger single-agent invocation, multi-agent planning, direct response, or safe escalation, while the second stage instantiates the selected action into executable outputs such as target agents, structured arguments, or multi-step plans. To adapt compact models to this setting, we further develop a routing-oriented fine-tuning scheme with candidate-aware supervision and hard negative examples. Experiments on a curated routing benchmark with several 3B--7B open-weight models show that compact models can provide competitive routing performance in constrained settings, and that model differences are mainly reflected in action prediction, candidate selection, and structured grounding quality. These results indicate that structured routing is a feasible design point for efficient and privacy-aware agent systems, especially when routing decisions must be made under resource-constrained deployment conditions.

### [192] [ATANT: An Evaluation Framework for AI Continuity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.06710)
*Samuel Sameer Tanguturi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ATANT是一个用于评估AI系统连续性能力的自动化测试框架，通过250个故事和1835个验证问题来衡量系统在时间维度上保持、更新、消歧和重建有意义上下文的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI行业已经开发了多种记忆组件（RAG管道、向量数据库、长上下文窗口、配置文件层），但缺乏正式框架来定义和测量这些组件是否产生真正的连续性。现有评估方法无法系统性地衡量AI系统在时间维度上保持上下文一致性的能力。

Method: 定义了连续性作为系统属性的7个必需特性，提出了包含10个检查点的评估方法（无需LLM参与评估循环），构建了包含250个故事、1835个验证问题的叙事测试语料库，涵盖6个生活领域。评估采用隔离模式和累积模式两种方式。

Result: 参考实现经过5次测试套件迭代，从58%（传统架构）提升到100%（隔离模式，250个故事）。在累积模式下，50个故事时达到100%，250个故事时达到96%。累积结果是主要衡量指标，要求系统在250个不同生活叙事共存时能正确检索事实而不发生交叉污染。

Conclusion: ATANT提供了一个系统无关、模型独立的连续性评估框架，作为构建和验证连续性系统的序列化方法。该框架能够正式定义和测量AI系统的连续性能力，填补了现有评估方法的空白。

Abstract: We present ATANT (Automated Test for Acceptance of Narrative Truth), an open evaluation framework for measuring continuity in AI systems: the ability to persist, update, disambiguate, and reconstruct meaningful context across time. While the AI industry has produced memory components (RAG pipelines, vector databases, long context windows, profile layers), no published framework formally defines or measures whether these components produce genuine continuity. We define continuity as a system property with 7 required properties, introduce a 10-checkpoint evaluation methodology that operates without an LLM in the evaluation loop, and present a narrative test corpus of 250 stories comprising 1,835 verification questions across 6 life domains. We evaluate a reference implementation across 5 test suite iterations, progressing from 58% (legacy architecture) to 100% in isolated mode (250 stories) and 100% in 50-story cumulative mode, with 96% at 250-story cumulative scale. The cumulative result is the primary measure: when 250 distinct life narratives coexist in the same database, the system must retrieve the correct fact for the correct context without cross-contamination. ATANT is system-agnostic, model-independent, and designed as a sequenced methodology for building and validating continuity systems. The framework specification, example stories, and evaluation protocol are available at https://github.com/Kenotic-Labs/ATANT. The full 250-story corpus will be released incrementally.

Abstract: AI applications driven by multimodal large language models (MLLMs) are prone to hallucinations and pose considerable risks to human users. Crucially, such hallucinations are not equally problematic: some hallucination contents could be detected by human users(i.e., obvious hallucinations), while others are often missed or require more verification effort(i.e., elusive hallucinations). This indicates that multimodal AI hallucinations vary significantly in their verifiability. Yet, little research has explored how to control this property for AI applications with diverse security and usability demands. To address this gap, we construct a dataset from 4,470 human responses to AI-generated hallucinations and categorize these hallucinations into obvious and elusive types based on their verifiability by human users. Further, we propose an activation-space intervention method that learns separate probes for obvious and elusive hallucinations. We reveal that obvious and elusive hallucinations elicit different intervention probes, allowing for fine-grained control over the model's verifiability. Empirical results demonstrate the efficacy of this approach and show that targeted interventions yield superior performance in regulating corresponding verifiability. Moreover, simply mixing these interventions enables flexible control over the verifiability required for different scenarios.

*Irina Arévalo,Marcos Oliva*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CAFP是一种模型无关的后处理方法，通过生成敏感属性翻转的反事实样本来平均预测结果，从而减少不公平性，无需重新训练或修改原始分类器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确保机器学习预测的公平性至关重要，特别是在信用评分、医疗保健和刑事司法等敏感领域。现有方法通常需要控制模型架构或访问受保护属性信息，这在现实系统中可能不可行。

Method: 提出Counterfactual Averaging for Fair Predictions (CAFP)，这是一种模型无关的后处理方法。对每个输入生成敏感属性翻转的反事实版本，然后平均原始模型在事实和反事实实例上的预测结果。

Result: 理论分析表明CAFP消除了对受保护属性的直接依赖，减少了预测与敏感属性之间的互信息，并界定了相对于原始模型的失真程度。在温和假设下，CAFP实现了完美的人口统计均等，并将均衡机会差距至少减少平均反事实偏差的一半。

Conclusion: CAFP提供了一种实用且理论上有保障的后处理方法，可在不修改原始模型的情况下减少机器学习预测中的不公平性，适用于现实世界系统。

Abstract: Ensuring fairness in machine learning predictions is a critical challenge, especially when models are deployed in sensitive domains such as credit scoring, healthcare, and criminal justice. While many fairness interventions rely on data preprocessing or algorithmic constraints during training, these approaches often require full control over the model architecture and access to protected attribute information, which may not be feasible in real-world systems. In this paper, we propose Counterfactual Averaging for Fair Predictions (CAFP), a model-agnostic post-processing method that mitigates unfair influence from protected attributes without retraining or modifying the original classifier. CAFP operates by generating counterfactual versions of each input in which the sensitive attribute is flipped, and then averaging the model's predictions across factual and counterfactual instances. We provide a theoretical analysis of CAFP, showing that it eliminates direct dependence on the protected attribute, reduces mutual information between predictions and sensitive attributes, and provably bounds the distortion introduced relative to the original model. Under mild assumptions, we further show that CAFP achieves perfect demographic parity and reduces the equalized odds gap by at least half the average counterfactual bias.

As a result, current resources provide limited support for testing whether a model can use remembered interaction history to interpret a user's present affective state.
  We introduce A-MBER, an Affective Memory Benchmark for Emotion Recognition, to evaluate this capability.   Experiments compare local-context, long-context, retrieved-memory, structured-memory, and gold-evidence conditions within a unified framework. Results show that A-MBER is especially discriminative on the subsets it is designed to stress, including long-range implicit affect, high-dependency memory levels, trajectory-based reasoning, and adversarial settings. These findings suggest that memory supports affective interpretation not simply by providing more history, but by enabling more selective, grounded, and context-sensitive use of past interaction

### [198] [Planning Task Shielding: Detecting and Repairing Flaws in Planning Tasks through Turning them Unsolvable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07042)
*Alberto Pozanco,Marianela Morales,Pietro Totis,Daniel Borrajo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出规划任务屏蔽（planning task shielding）概念，通过检测和修复规划任务中的缺陷，使包含不可达状态的规划任务变得不可解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统规划研究主要关注生成达成目标的计划，但目标规范也可用于编码不应成立的性质，从而识别导致缺陷状态的轨迹。当规划任务包含应避免的缺陷状态时，目标转变为修改规划任务以确保缺陷状态永不达到，即使规划任务不可解。

Method: 提出$allmin$算法，通过最小化修改原始动作来使规划任务不可解，从而解决规划任务屏蔽问题。该算法是最优的。

Result: 通过实验评估$allmin$在不同规模规划任务中的性能，证明其能有效屏蔽系统，使规划任务不可解。

Conclusion: 规划任务屏蔽是规划领域的重要扩展，$allmin$算法能有效检测和修复规划任务中的缺陷，通过最小化修改确保系统安全。

Abstract: Most research in planning focuses on generating a plan to achieve a desired set of goals. However, a goal specification can also be used to encode a property that should never hold, allowing a planner to identify a trace that would reach a flawed state. In such cases, the objective may shift to modifying the planning task to ensure that the flawed state is never reached-in other words, to make the planning task unsolvable. In this paper we introduce planning task shielding: the problem of detecting and repairing flaws in planning tasks. We propose $allmin$, an optimal algorithm that solves these tasks by minimally modifying the original actions to render the planning task unsolvable. We empirically evaluate the performance of $allmin$ in shielding planning tasks of increasing size, showing how it can effectively shield the system by turning the planning task unsolvable.

</details>


### [199] [EVGeoQA: Benchmarking LLMs on Dynamic, Multi-Objective Geo-Spatial Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07070)
*Jianfei Wu,Zhichun Wang,Zhensheng Wang,Zhiyu He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: EVGeoQA是一个基于电动汽车充电场景的新型地理空间问答基准，具有位置锚定和双目标设计，用于评估LLM在动态地理环境中的目的驱动探索能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有地理空间问答基准主要关注静态检索，无法捕捉涉及动态用户位置和复合约束的真实世界规划复杂性。需要评估LLM在动态地理环境中的目的驱动探索能力。

Method: 提出EVGeoQA基准，基于电动汽车充电场景，具有位置锚定和双目标设计（充电需求+协同活动偏好）。进一步提出GeoRover评估框架，基于工具增强的智能体架构来评估LLM的动态多目标探索能力。

Result: 实验表明LLM能成功利用工具处理子任务，但在长距离空间探索方面存在困难。观察到涌现能力：LLM能总结历史探索轨迹以提升探索效率。

Conclusion: EVGeoQA为未来地理空间智能提供了一个具有挑战性的测试平台，揭示了LLM在动态地理环境探索中的能力与局限。

Abstract: While Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable reasoning capabilities, their potential for purpose-driven exploration in dynamic geo-spatial environments remains under-investigated. Existing Geo-Spatial Question Answering (GSQA) benchmarks predominantly focus on static retrieval, failing to capture the complexity of real-world planning that involves dynamic user locations and compound constraints. To bridge this gap, we introduce EVGeoQA, a novel benchmark built upon Electric Vehicle (EV) charging scenarios that features a distinct location-anchored and dual-objective design. Specifically, each query in EVGeoQA is explicitly bound to a user's real-time coordinate and integrates the dual objectives of a charging necessity and a co-located activity preference. To systematically assess models in such complex settings, we further propose GeoRover, a general evaluation framework based on a tool-augmented agent architecture to evaluate the LLMs' capacity for dynamic, multi-objective exploration. Our experiments reveal that while LLMs successfully utilize tools to address sub-tasks, they struggle with long-range spatial exploration. Notably, we observe an emergent capability: LLMs can summarize historical exploration trajectories to enhance exploration efficiency. These findings establish EVGeoQA as a challenging testbed for future geo-spatial intelligence. The dataset and prompts are available at https://github.com/Hapluckyy/EVGeoQA/.

</details>


### [200] [Reason in Chains, Learn in Trees: Self-Rectification and Grafting for Multi-turn Agent Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07165)
*Yu Li,Sizhe Tang,Tian Lan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: T-STAR通过构建认知树识别关键推理步骤，利用回溯估值机制传播轨迹级奖励，并通过上下文思维嫁接合成纠正推理，在需要长推理链的任务上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法（如GRPO）将采样的轨迹视为独立链，对所有步骤分配均匀信用，忽视了关键步骤对推理结果的非对称影响，导致稀疏奖励问题在LLM多步推理任务中难以解决。

Method: 提出T-STAR框架：1）将轨迹整合为统一的认知树，识别并合并功能相似的步骤/节点；2）引入回溯估值机制，通过树结构反向传播轨迹级奖励，获得方差减少的步骤级相对优势；3）开发上下文思维嫁接，通过对比成功与失败分支在关键分歧点的差异合成纠正推理；4）提出外科手术式策略优化，利用Bradley-Terry类型的外科损失在关键点集中利用策略梯度信息。

Result: 在具身、交互、推理和规划基准上的广泛实验表明，T-STAR相比强基线实现了一致的改进，在需要扩展推理链的任务上增益最为显著。

Conclusion: T-STAR通过恢复看似独立轨迹间的潜在相关奖励结构，有效解决了多步推理中的稀疏奖励问题，通过认知树结构识别关键步骤并集中优化，显著提升了LLM智能体的推理性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning for Large Language Model agents is often hindered by sparse rewards in multi-step reasoning tasks. Existing approaches like Group Relative Policy Optimization treat sampled trajectories as independent chains, assigning uniform credit to all steps in each chain and ignoring the existence of critical steps that may disproportionally impact reasoning outcome. In this paper, we propose T-STAR(Tree-structured Self-Taught Agent Rectification), a framework that recovers the latent correlated reward structure across seemingly independent trajectories. Specifically, we consolidate trajectories into a unified Cognitive Tree by identifying and merging functionally similar steps/nodes. It enables an Introspective Valuation mechanism that back-propagates trajectory-level rewards through the tree to obtain a new notion of variance-reduced relative advantage at step-level. Using the Cognitive Tree, we also develop In-Context Thought Grafting to synthesize corrective reasoning by contrasting successful and failed branches at critical divergence points/steps. Our proposed Surgical Policy Optimization then capitalizes on the rich policy gradient information concentrated at these critical points/steps through a Bradley-Terry type of surgical loss. Extensive experiments across embodied, interactive, reasoning, and planning benchmarks demonstrate that T-STAR achieves consistent improvements over strong baselines, with gains most pronounced on tasks requiring extended reasoning chains.

</details>


### [201] [How Much LLM Does a Self-Revising Agent Actually Need?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.07236)
*Seongwoo Jeong,Seonil Son*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种声明式反射运行时协议，将智能体状态、置信信号、防护动作和假设转换外部化为可检查的运行时结构，用于分解LLM智能体能力来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于LLM的智能体通常将世界建模、规划和反思放在单一语言模型循环中，这使得难以区分智能体能力中哪些来自LLM本身，哪些来自其周围的结构化设计。

Method: 引入声明式反射运行时协议，将智能体状态、置信信号、防护动作和假设转换外部化为可检查的运行时结构。在Collaborative Battleship任务上实例化该协议，使用四种渐进结构化的智能体进行54轮游戏评估。

Result: 分解出四个组件：后验信念跟踪、显式世界模型规划、符号化回合内反思和稀疏LLM修订。显式世界模型规划相比贪婪后验跟踪基线显著提升（+24.1%胜率，+0.017 F1）。符号化反思作为实际运行时机制运行，但当前修订预设尚未产生净正收益。在约4.3%回合添加条件性LLM修订仅产生微小非单调变化。

Conclusion: 外部化反思将原本潜在的智能体行为转化为可检查的运行时结构，使LLM干预的边际作用能够被直接研究，这是方法论贡献而非性能领先声明。

Abstract: Recent LLM-based agents often place world modeling, planning, and reflection inside a single language model loop. This can produce capable behavior, but it makes a basic scientific question difficult to answer: which part of the agent's competence actually comes from the LLM, and which part comes from explicit structure around it?
  We study this question not by claiming a general answer, but by making it empirically tractable. We introduce a declared reflective runtime protocol that externalizes agent state, confidence signals, guarded actions, and hypothetical transitions into inspectable runtime structure. We instantiate this protocol in a declarative runtime and evaluate it on noisy Collaborative Battleship [4] using four progressively structured agents over 54 games (18 boards $\times$ 3 seeds).
  The resulting decomposition isolates four components: posterior belief tracking, explicit world-model planning, symbolic in-episode reflection, and sparse LLM-based revision. Across this decomposition, explicit world-model planning improves substantially over a greedy posterior-following baseline (+24.1pp win rate, +0.017 F1). Symbolic reflection operates as a real runtime mechanism -- with prediction tracking, confidence gating, and guarded revision actions -- even though its current revision presets are not yet net-positive in aggregate. Adding conditional LLM revision at about 4.3\% of turns yields only a small and non-monotonic change: average F1 rises slightly (+0.005) while win rate drops (31$\rightarrow$29 out of 54).
  These results suggest a methodological contribution rather than a leaderboard claim: externalizing reflection turns otherwise latent agent behavior into inspectable runtime structure, allowing the marginal role of LLM intervention to be studied directly.

</details>
